 mallik ne bataaya ki mangalvaar ko ralospa ke rashtriya adhyaksh or kendriya maanav sansaadhan vikaas rajya mantri upendra kushvaha ko piem modi ne milane ke liye bulaayaa tha

 aise main AAP pratyaashee kumaar vishwaas hi rahul gandhi ke liye ekmaatr prakat chunauti ke rup main dikh rahe hai
 Kumar started living in Amethi even before his candidature was announced
 ek maheene se vah lagaataar amethi main gum-gum kar prachaar kar rahe hai
 Poet-turned-politician Kumar Vishwas is trying to make development in Amethi, Rahul Gandhi's 'vadakhilafi' and familyism an election issue
 lekin ek mudda he jis par unhen hathonhaath sthaneey logon kaa samarthan mil rahaa he
 That is the plight of Amethi roads
 khaas taur se vah sadak jo raibareli tak jaati he
 Kumar is well aware that the people of Amethi are troubled by the plight of the roads, so they do not miss making it an election issue
 haal hi main unhone kaha tha, 'mahilaon ne mujhe bataaya ki raibareli or amethi ke bich sadak kii haalat itani kharaab he ki gaddhon kii vajah se hi ek darjan se zyada mahilaon kii delivery ho gai
 'though the people of Amethi are waiting for the support and gesture of Kumar Vishwas, it does not appear
 haalanki jab ham amethi se raibareli kii taraf bade, to logon main gusse kii vajah saaf hoti gai
 The road from Gauriganj to Fursatganj via Bahadurpur has almost disappeared due to lack of good construction and maintenance
 sthaneey log is bare main rahul ko kai baar yaad dilaa chuke hai
 Surprisingly, Rahul's subordinate leader presents a completely different picture of Amethi
 amethi ke congress jiladhyaksh yogendra mishra ne sadak banavaane ke liye aavantit kii gai rakam kii jaankaree di
 According to the party's estimate, around Rs 800 crore was spent to build and repair the 240-km long National Highway passing through Amethi
